\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_call\_function()}{wb\_call\_function()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+call\+\_\+function (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$address,  }\item[{}]{\$args = {\ttfamily \mbox{[}\mbox{]}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Calls the D\+LL function pointed by address. args is an optional array of parameters that must match those of the function being called. Returns an integer that may be a valid value or a pointer to one object, according to the library function called.

N\+O\+TE\+: Function arguments are limited to a maximum of 20.

\index{winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}!wb\_create\_font@{wb\_create\_font}}
\index{wb\_create\_font@{wb\_create\_font}!winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_create\_font()}{wb\_create\_font()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+create\+\_\+font (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$name,  }\item[{}]{\$height,  }\item[{}]{\$color = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$flags = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a new font. name is the font name, height is its height in points (not pixels), and color is a R\+GB color value. flags can be a combination of the following values\+:.

F\+T\+A\+\_\+\+N\+O\+R\+M\+AL F\+T\+A\+\_\+\+R\+E\+G\+U\+L\+AR F\+T\+A\+\_\+\+B\+O\+LD F\+T\+A\+\_\+\+I\+T\+A\+L\+IC F\+T\+A\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+E\+R\+L\+I\+NE F\+T\+A\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+K\+E\+O\+UT

Constants of F\+T\+A\+\_\+\+N\+O\+R\+M\+AL and F\+T\+A\+\_\+\+R\+E\+G\+U\+L\+AR mean the same thing and are defined as zero.

The function returns an integer value that is the font identifier.

After use, the font must be destroyed by a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a6d77b990318851a862ee50b1220c3b3a}{wb\+\_\+destroy\+\_\+font()}} to prevent resource leaks.

N\+O\+TE\+: The color parameter is not implemented yet.

Creates a transparency mask of a true-\/color bitmap. The mask returned is also a bitmap. The transparent color is set by transparent\+\_\+color.

N\+O\+TE\+: The resulting image must be destroyed by a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a119b029ffa03d6f2ea1fefd46997b9ee}{wb\+\_\+destroy\+\_\+image()}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{winbinder_8php_a71b61ba0792bda0516e4f4c2202da09d}\label{winbinder_8php_a71b61ba0792bda0516e4f4c2202da09d}} 
\index{winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}!wb\_create\_timer@{wb\_create\_timer}}
\index{wb\_create\_timer@{wb\_create\_timer}!winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_create\_timer()}{wb\_create\_timer()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+create\+\_\+timer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$window,  }\item[{}]{\$id,  }\item[{}]{\$interval }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a timer in the specified window. The timer must be given an integer id that must be unique to all timers and controls. interval specifies the time-\/out value in milliseconds. Timer events are passed to and processed by the window callback function. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} call to \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_aba7673cad1aa4ea3da720a561eb29b05}{wb\+\_\+destroy\+\_\+timer()}} destroys the timer.

Low resolution and high resolution timers

This function supports both conventional (low-\/resolution) and multimedia (high-\/resolution) timers. Use a non-\/negative id to specify a low-\/resolution timer or a negative id to specify a high-\/resolution timer. Hi-\/res timers have a 10\+:1 increase in speed (resolution can go down to 1 ms opposed to 10 ms of a conventional timer) and much higher precision.

N\+O\+TE\+: Only one high-\/resolution timer is allowed per application and it must be on the main window.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em \$window} & \\
\hline
{\em \$id} & \\
\hline
{\em \$interval} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_create\_window()}{wb\_create\_window()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+create\+\_\+window (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$parent,  }\item[{}]{\$wclass,  }\item[{}]{\$caption = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$xpos = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$ypos = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$width = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$height = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$param = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a window of class wclass. Click here for a list of the available window classes. Windows created with this function must be destroyed with a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a5a0b5719b16ae952aa77f984a454c0c2}{wb\+\_\+destroy\+\_\+window()}}. Optional style flags may be passed through parameter style. To enable additional messages in a particular window, include the W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+I\+FY style in the style parameter and use param to indicate which additional notification messages you want to process.

This function may set the text and/or the tooltip (small hint window) of the window when it is created. To create a tooltip, text must be an array with two elements. The first one is the new caption (or N\+U\+LL if one is not required) and the second one is the new tooltip (or N\+U\+LL if one is not required). All classes support tooltips.

Returns the handle of the newly created window or N\+U\+LL or zero if an error occurs.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_delete\_items()}{wb\_delete\_items()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+delete\+\_\+items (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$ctrl,  }\item[{}]{\$items = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Deletes an item, a range of items, or all items from a control. Returns T\+R\+UE on success or F\+A\+L\+SE if an error occurs. Control classes.

This function applies to the following control classes\+: List\+Box, Combo\+Box, List\+View and Tree\+View.

\$items can be\+: integer Deletes the specified item. array of integers Deletes the specified items. zero Deletes item zero. null Deletes all items.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+draw\+\_\+ellipse (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$target,  }\item[{}]{\$xpos,  }\item[{}]{\$ypos,  }\item[{}]{\$width,  }\item[{}]{\$height,  }\item[{}]{\$color,  }\item[{}]{\$filled = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$linewidth = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$linestyle = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws a filled or hollow rectangle. The first parameter, target, may be a Win\+Binder object, a window handle, a drawing surface or a bitmap.

xpos and ypos are the coordinates of the upper-\/left corner of the rectangle, in pixels. width and height are the dimensions of the rectangle. color is a R\+GB color value. Set filled to F\+A\+L\+SE to draw a border. In this case, linewidth sets the width of the border, in pixels. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} linewidth of zero sets the width to 1 pixel.

Returns T\+R\+UE on success or F\+A\+L\+SE if an error occurs.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_draw\_image()}{wb\_draw\_image()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+draw\+\_\+image (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$target,  }\item[{}]{\$bitmap,  }\item[{}]{\$xpos = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$ypos = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$width = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$height = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$transparentcolor = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$xoffset = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$yoffset = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws a bitmap. The first parameter, target, may be a Win\+Binder object, a window handle, a drawing surface or another bitmap.

xpos and ypos are the coordinates of the upper-\/left corner, in pixels. These parameters default to zero. width and height are the dimensions of the rectangle. These parameters also default to zero. In this case the bitmap is drawn with its original size. The parameter transparentcolor may be used to indicate which color is to be made transparent. If is set to N\+O\+C\+O\+L\+OR (the default), no transparency is used and the image is opaque. Parameters xoffset and yoffset are optionally used to specify where the image will be drawn.

Returns T\+R\+UE on success or F\+A\+L\+SE if an error occurs.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+draw\+\_\+line (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$target,  }\item[{}]{\$x0,  }\item[{}]{\$y0,  }\item[{}]{\$x1,  }\item[{}]{\$y1,  }\item[{}]{\$color,  }\item[{}]{\$linewidth = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$linestyle = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws a straight line. The first parameter, target, may be a Win\+Binder object, a window handle, a drawing surface or a bitmap.

The start and end points of the line are (x0, y0) and (x1, y1) respectively, in pixels. color is a R\+GB color value and linewidth is the width of the line, in pixels. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} linewidth of zero sets the width to 1 pixel. Parameter linestyle accepts the values specified in the table below.

0 Solid line (the default style) 1 Dotted line 2-\/7 Dashed lines with increasing lengths 8 Line with alternating dashes and dots 9 Line with alternating dashes and double dots

Returns T\+R\+UE on success or F\+A\+L\+SE if an error occurs.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+draw\+\_\+text (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$target,  }\item[{}]{\$text,  }\item[{}]{\$xpos,  }\item[{}]{\$ypos,  }\item[{}]{\$width = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$height = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$font = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$flags = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws a string. The first parameter, target, may be a Win\+Binder object, a window handle, a drawing surface or a bitmap.

The text parameter is the string to be drawn. xpos and ypos are the coordinates of the upper-\/left corner, in pixels. width and height optionally provide a limit to the drawing area. If they are not provided or zero, there is no limit to the drawing area. To use a specific font, an identifier created with \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_afb7b299b3703d5b05be81ec46fb6917d}{wb\+\_\+create\+\_\+font()}} must be used as the font argument. If font is N\+U\+LL, negative or not given, the most recently created font is used.

N\+O\+TE\+: To use the simplified call syntax (no width, no height) you must supply 4 or 5 parameters.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{winbinder_8php_a972a5903cf22b19b1e1f03cc51654d37}\label{winbinder_8php_a972a5903cf22b19b1e1f03cc51654d37}} 
\index{winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}!wb\_get\_function\_address@{wb\_get\_function\_address}}
\index{wb\_get\_function\_address@{wb\_get\_function\_address}!winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_get\_function\_address()}{wb\_get\_function\_address()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+get\+\_\+function\+\_\+address (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$fname,  }\item[{}]{\$idlib }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the address of a library function. fname is the function name and idlib identifies a library already loaded. The idlib identifier must have been obtained with a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a1de04890549b712326f8974429753bcc}{wb\+\_\+load\+\_\+library()}}. If idlib is not set or is set to N\+U\+LL, the last library sent to the function will be used.

Name expansion\+: The function prepends and appends some special characters to the function name until it finds the function name, then it returns the function address or N\+U\+LL if the function was not found. These special characters are the most common ones encountered in various types of libraries.

For example, if fname is set to \char`\"{}\+My\+Function\char`\"{}, \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a972a5903cf22b19b1e1f03cc51654d37}{wb\+\_\+get\+\_\+function\+\_\+address()}} looks for the following function names, in order\+:

My\+Function My\+FunctionA My\+FunctionW \+\_\+\+My\+Function \+\_\+\+My\+FunctionA \+\_\+\+My\+FunctionW My\+Function@0, My\+Function@4, My\+Function@8... until My\+Function@80 \+\_\+\+My\+Function@0, \+\_\+\+My\+Function@4, \+\_\+\+My\+Function@8... until My\+Function@80

The last two expansion options include a \textquotesingle{}@\textquotesingle{} character followed by the number of parameters times 4, which is a standard way to store function names inside D\+L\+Ls. The loop starts from zero (\char`\"{}@0\char`\"{}) and ends when it reaches 20 parameters (\char`\"{}@80\char`\"{}).

N\+O\+TE\+: Function names, including the expansion characters, are limited to 255 characters.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em \$fname} & \\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{winbinder_8php_a4479398989d3bd93f21545d6f9a04d9d}\label{winbinder_8php_a4479398989d3bd93f21545d6f9a04d9d}} 
\index{winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}!wb\_get\_instance@{wb\_get\_instance}}
\index{wb\_get\_instance@{wb\_get\_instance}!winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_get\_instance()}{wb\_get\_instance()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+get\+\_\+instance (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$caption,  }\item[{}]{\$bringtofront = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Detects a running instance of a Win\+Binder application.

Detecting running instances

Each main window of all Win\+Binder applications stores a 32-\/bit identifier that is calculated according to the initial window caption and is unique to that caption. \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a4479398989d3bd93f21545d6f9a04d9d}{wb\+\_\+get\+\_\+instance()}} will try to find, among all current top-\/level windows, a Win\+Binder window that was created with the same caption. The function returns T\+R\+UE if it finds the existing window or F\+A\+L\+SE if it is does not.

The function is effective even of the caption of the first instance of the application is changed at runtime because the 32-\/bit identifier does not change throughout the life of the application.

If bringtofront is set to T\+R\+UE, the function optionally restores the window (if minimized) and brings the corresponding window to the front of other windows.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em \$caption} & \\
\hline
null & {\em \$bringtofront} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
bool 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}!wb\_get\_registry\_key@{wb\_get\_registry\_key}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_get\_registry\_key()}{wb\_get\_registry\_key()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+get\+\_\+registry\+\_\+key (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$key,  }\item[{}]{\$subkey,  }\item[{}]{\$entry = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reads a string or integer value from the Windows registry item referenced by key, subkey and entry. The subkey may contain forward or reverse slashes. If entry is an empty string, a N\+U\+LL value or is not supplied, the function retrieves the default value for the subkey.

Values are always returned as strings. If the requested entry is an empty string, an empty string is returned. If the key does not exist in the registry, the function returns N\+U\+LL.

Returns a value or array with the indices or identifiers of the selected elements or items in wbobject.

Retrives\+:

\mbox{\Hypertarget{winbinder_8php_aec93dfc272173333e8819697e22fedda}\label{winbinder_8php_aec93dfc272173333e8819697e22fedda}} 
\index{winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}!wb\_get\_size@{wb\_get\_size}}
\index{wb\_get\_size@{wb\_get\_size}!winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_get\_size()}{wb\_get\_size()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+get\+\_\+size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$object,  }\item[{}]{\$param = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Gets the dimensions of a control, window, image or string. The image handle must have been obtained with \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a2ee8c2c296bacec8f9b974fe885d61c3}{wb\+\_\+create\+\_\+image()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a84052afa9ab3c2f16410a6350aee67b1}{wb\+\_\+create\+\_\+mask()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a13bbb316c4fba26e8cff4976fc3d05f5}{wb\+\_\+load\+\_\+image()}}.

This function generally returns an array where the first element is the width and the second is the height. Measurements are in pixels. If param is T\+R\+UE, the area returned will not include the title bar and borders. Default is F\+A\+L\+SE.

The function will return the integer W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+ED instead of an array if the requested window is minimized, or N\+U\+LL on error.

If object is a List\+View handle and param is T\+R\+UE, the function returns an array with the widths of the column headers. If param is omitted or F\+A\+L\+SE, the function behaves normally like described above

If object is a text string, param is optionally used to pass the handle to a font created with \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_afb7b299b3703d5b05be81ec46fb6917d}{wb\+\_\+create\+\_\+font()}}. If param is null or not used, the default font is used. Object types accepted

object may be one of the following\+:

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} control handle \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} window handle An icon handle \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} bitmap handle The name of a bitmap file The name of an icon file \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} text string


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em \$object} & \\
\hline
null & {\em \$param} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
array 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+get\+\_\+system\+\_\+info (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$info }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns information about the current system and application, according to the string info.

The parameter info is not case-\/sensitive.

\char`\"{}appmemory\char`\"{} The total memory used by the application¹ \char`\"{}backgroundcolor\char`\"{} The main face color for Windows dialog boxes and controls \char`\"{}colordepth\char`\"{} The current color depth in bits per pixel \char`\"{}commandline\char`\"{} The original Windows command line including the executable file \char`\"{}computername\char`\"{} The name of the computer inside the~network \char`\"{}consolemode\char`\"{} 1 indicates that console mode~(D\+OS box) is active, 0 otherwise \char`\"{}diskdrives\char`\"{} The list of all available disk drives \char`\"{}exepath\char`\"{} The path to the main executable (P\+H\+P.\+E\+XE) \char`\"{}fontpath\char`\"{} The current font path \char`\"{}freememory\char`\"{} The available physical memory \char`\"{}gdiobjects\char`\"{} The number of currently allocated G\+DI handles \char`\"{}instance\char`\"{} The instance identifier of the current application \char`\"{}osnumber\char`\"{} The numeric OS version number \char`\"{}ospath\char`\"{} The current OS path \char`\"{}osversion\char`\"{} The complete OS version name \char`\"{}pgmpath\char`\"{} The default OS application path \char`\"{}screenarea\char`\"{} The total area (x, y, width, height) of the screen, in pixels \char`\"{}systemfont\char`\"{} The common (default) system font for dialog boxes \char`\"{}systempath\char`\"{} The OS system path \char`\"{}temppath\char`\"{} The path used by the OS to hold temporary files \char`\"{}totalmemory\char`\"{} The total physical memory installed \char`\"{}username\char`\"{} The name of the currently logged user \char`\"{}userobjects\char`\"{} The number of currently allocated U\+S\+ER handles \char`\"{}workarea\char`\"{} The valid area (x, y, width, height) of the screen, in pixels

\index{wb\_load\_image@{wb\_load\_image}!winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_load\_image()}{wb\_load\_image()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+load\+\_\+image (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$filename,  }\item[{}]{\$index = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$param = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Loads the image, icon or cursor file filename from disk and returns a handle to it. If filename is an icon library, index specifies the index of the image inside the file. Default index is 0.

If source is an icon or a cursor, if param is 0 (the default), the function returns a large icon or cursor if param is 1, it returns a small icon or cursor; if param is -\/1, the function returns the default icon or cursor.

N\+O\+TE\+: The resulting image must be destroyed by a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a119b029ffa03d6f2ea1fefd46997b9ee}{wb\+\_\+destroy\+\_\+image()}}.

\index{wb\_load\_library@{wb\_load\_library}!winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_load\_library()}{wb\_load\_library()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+load\+\_\+library (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$libname }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Loads a D\+LL into memory. Returns an integer identifying libname. If libname is N\+U\+LL then returns the identifier of the last library returned. The function accepts fully qualified and raw names. Returns N\+U\+LL if no library was found.

Name expansion

The function appends some characters to the library name until it finds the library, then it returns an identifier for that library, or N\+U\+LL if the library was not found. If libname is \char`\"{}\+L\+I\+B\char`\"{}, for example, the function looks for the following files, in order\+:

L\+IB L\+I\+B.\+D\+LL L\+I\+B32 L\+I\+B32.\+D\+LL L\+I\+B.\+E\+XE L\+I\+B32.\+E\+XE

For each name, the function looks in the following locations\+:

The application directory; The current directory; The 32-\/bit System directory (Usually C\+:\textbackslash{}\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+WS\textbackslash{}\+S\+Y\+S\+T\+E\+M32 or C\+:\textbackslash{}\+W\+I\+N\+NT\textbackslash{}\+S\+Y\+S\+T\+E\+M32); The 16-\/bit System directory (Usually C\+:\textbackslash{}\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+WS\textbackslash{}\+S\+Y\+S\+T\+EM or C\+:\textbackslash{}\+W\+I\+N\+NT\textbackslash{}\+S\+Y\+S\+T\+EM); The Windows directory (Usually C\+:\textbackslash{}\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+WS or C\+:\textbackslash{}\+W\+I\+N\+NT); The directory list contained in the P\+A\+TH environment variable.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em \$libname} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
int 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{winbinder_8php_aab78c3a24a89378841164f5e788caa60}\label{winbinder_8php_aab78c3a24a89378841164f5e788caa60}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+message\+\_\+box (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$parent,  }\item[{}]{\$message,  }\item[{}]{\$title = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates and displays a message box under the style supplied and returns a value according to the button pressed.

Value for style \& What is displayed

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+OK (the default) -\/ An OK button.

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+FO -\/ An information icon and an OK button.

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG -\/ An exclamation point icon and an OK button.

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+S\+T\+OP -\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} stop icon and an OK button.

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+S\+T\+I\+ON -\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} question mark icon and an OK button.

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+O\+K\+C\+A\+N\+C\+EL -\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} question mark icon, an OK button and a Cancel button.

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+Y\+E\+S\+NO -\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} question mark icon, a Yes button and a No button.

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+Y\+E\+S\+N\+O\+C\+A\+N\+C\+EL -\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} question mark icon, a Yes button, a No button and a Cancel button.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{winbinder_8php_a3d5e6ee924052b8743d8f0b31e0e1fe9}\label{winbinder_8php_a3d5e6ee924052b8743d8f0b31e0e1fe9}} 
\index{winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}!wb\_play\_sound@{wb\_play\_sound}}
\index{wb\_play\_sound@{wb\_play\_sound}!winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_play\_sound()}{wb\_play\_sound()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+play\+\_\+sound (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$source,  }\item[{}]{\$command = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Loads and plays a sound file or system sound. Parameter source may be a sound file name or a system sound constant. Parameter command may be used used to play a W\+AV sound synchronously or in a loop. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} synchronous sound stops the currently playing sound and suspends the application control until it finishes. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} M\+I\+DI soundtrack always stops any currenly playing M\+I\+DI soundtrack. To stop one or more sounds, use function \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a803040b4a460651c9bcb4e2f654ed4f9}{wb\+\_\+stop\+\_\+sound()}}.

Value of \$source\+: M\+I\+DI file name -\/ Load and play the specified M\+I\+DI file.

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+OK -\/ Default system sound

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+FO -\/ System information sound

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG -\/ Warning sound

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+S\+T\+OP -\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_error}{Error}} sound

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+S\+T\+I\+ON -\/ Question sound

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+B\+E\+EP -\/ Default beep (via the computer speaker)

Value of \$command\+: null or empty -\/ Load and play the specified W\+AV sound file.

\textquotesingle{}sync\textquotesingle{} -\/ Load and play the specified W\+AV sound file synchronously.

\textquotesingle{}loop\textquotesingle{} -\/ Load and loop the specified W\+AV sound file.

Returns T\+R\+UE on success or F\+A\+L\+SE otherwise.

null & {\em \$command} & \\

{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+refresh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$wbobject,  }\item[{}]{\$now = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$xpos = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$ypos = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$width = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$height = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Refreshes or redraws the Win\+Binder object wbobject, forcing an immediate redraw if the parameter now is T\+R\+UE (the default). If now is F\+A\+L\+SE, the redraw command is posted to the Windows message queue.

Optional parameters xpos, ypos, width and height will make the function invalidate and redraw only the specified part of the screen or control.

Returns T\+R\+UE on success or F\+A\+L\+SE if an error occurs.

0x\+F\+F\+FF

This constant is the value of H\+W\+N\+D\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+ST in the Windows A\+PI. For more information consult the Windows A\+PI documentation.

Sets a specific area in a window. Possible values for type are\+:.

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+T\+I\+T\+LE Sets the area used to drag a borderless window with the mouse.

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+S\+I\+ZE Sets the minimum window size in a resizable window. Parameters x and y are ignored. If width is zero, no minimum horizontal dimension is set. if height is zero, no minimum vertical dimension is set.

W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+S\+I\+ZE Sets the maximum window size in a resizable window. Parameters x and y are ignored. If width is zero, no maximum horizontal dimension is set. if height is zero, no maximum vertical dimension is set.

The source parameter can be a cursor handle from function \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a13bbb316c4fba26e8cff4976fc3d05f5}{wb\+\_\+load\+\_\+image()}} or one of the preset system cursors\+: arrow, cross, finger, forbidden, help, ibeam, null (no cursor), sizeall, sizenesw, sizens, sizenwse, sizewe, uparrow, wait and waitarrow.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_set\_font()}{wb\_set\_font()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+set\+\_\+font (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$control,  }\item[{}]{\$font = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$redraw = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the font of control. font is a unique integer value returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_afb7b299b3703d5b05be81ec46fb6917d}{wb\+\_\+create\+\_\+font()}}. If font is zero or not given, the most recently created font is used. If font is a negative number, it means the system default font.

Returns T\+R\+UE on success or F\+A\+L\+SE if an error occurs.

Tip\+: To check the system font name and size, call \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a262b5f78446536ef9b8affb993303f33}{wb\+\_\+get\+\_\+system\+\_\+info()}} using (\char`\"{}systemfont\char`\"{}) as the info parameter.

\index{winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}!wb\_set\_handler@{wb\_set\_handler}}
\index{wb\_set\_handler@{wb\_set\_handler}!winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_set\_handler()}{wb\_set\_handler()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+set\+\_\+handler (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$window,  }\item[{}]{\$fn\+\_\+handler }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Assigns the callback function fn\+\_\+handler to window. The handler function may be a regular P\+HP function or class method that is used to process events for this particular window. \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a2c420d93bb39e83260cf90c5552580a9}{wb\+\_\+set\+\_\+handler()}} must be called whenever the window needs to process messages and events from its controls.

To specify a function as the handler, pass the function name in fn\+\_\+handler. If the handler is a class method, fn\+\_\+handler must be an array which first element is the name of the object and the second one is the method name.

For additional information, see callback functions and window handlers.

\index{wb\_set\_image@{wb\_set\_image}!winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_set\_image()}{wb\_set\_image()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+set\+\_\+image (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$wbobject,  }\item[{}]{\$source,  }\item[{}]{\$transparentcolor = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$index = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$param = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Assigns the image source to the Win\+Binder object wbobject. Parameter source can be either an image, icon or cursor handle or a path to an image file name. If a handle, it must have been obtained with \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a2ee8c2c296bacec8f9b974fe885d61c3}{wb\+\_\+create\+\_\+image()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a84052afa9ab3c2f16410a6350aee67b1}{wb\+\_\+create\+\_\+mask()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a13bbb316c4fba26e8cff4976fc3d05f5}{wb\+\_\+load\+\_\+image()}}. The optional parameter transparentcolor tells the function which color is to be considered transparent. The default is N\+O\+C\+O\+L\+OR (no transparency). index is used to select a specific image from a multi-\/image file (such as a D\+LL or executable).

If source is an icon or a cursor, if param is 0 (the default), the function sets a large icon or cursor. if param is 1, it sets a small icon or cursor; if param is -\/1, the function sets the default icon or cursor. For minimized windows, this function will also change the icon that is displayed on the task bar.

Returns T\+R\+UE on success or F\+A\+L\+SE if an error occurs.

\hline

null & {\em \$index} & \\
\hline
null & {\em \$param} & \\

{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+set\+\_\+item\+\_\+image (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$wbobject,  }\item[{}]{\$index,  }\item[{}]{\$item = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$subitem = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Retrieves a portion of the image already assigned to a control and assigns it to a item (and optional subitem). The image must be previously assigned with \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_a5d403a35eefd4c58a0831085fb5e3e8a}{wb\+\_\+set\+\_\+image()}}. The portion which is assigned is specified by index.

Returns T\+R\+UE on success or F\+A\+L\+SE if an error occurs.

\char`\"{}cmd\+:back\char`\"{} Go to previously visited page. \char`\"{}cmd\+:forward\char`\"{} Go to a page previously viewed before issuing the back command. \char`\"{}cmd\+:refresh\char`\"{} Redraw the current page. \char`\"{}cmd\+:stop\char`\"{} Stop the current action, like loading a page. \char`\"{}cmd\+:busy\char`\"{} Return T\+R\+UE if the browser is busy or F\+A\+L\+SE if idle. \char`\"{}cmd\+:blank\char`\"{} Clear the page.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_set\_registry\_key()}{wb\_set\_registry\_key()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+set\+\_\+registry\+\_\+key (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$key,  }\item[{}]{\$subkey,  }\item[{}]{\$entry = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$value = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reads a string or integer value from the Windows registry item referenced by key, subkey and entry. The subkey may contain forward or reverse slashes. If entry is an empty string, a N\+U\+LL value or is not supplied, the function retrieves the default value for the subkey.

Values are always returned as strings. If the requested entry is an empty string, an empty string is returned. If the key does not exist in the registry, the function returns N\+U\+LL.

\index{wb\_sort@{wb\_sort}!winbinder.php@{winbinder.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_sort()}{wb\_sort()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+sort (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$control,  }\item[{}]{\$ascending = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$subitem = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sorts the contents of a control, a control item, a List\+View column or a sub-\/item. If the ascending parameter is T\+R\+UE (the default), the control or column is ordered starting with the lowest value or string, and vice-\/versa.

The sorting criteria between two given items, item1 and item2, are as follows\+:

String or number String Alphabetical order according to system locale String or number Empty The non-\/empty item is always greater than the empty one Number Number Numeric comparison

In a List\+View, \mbox{\hyperlink{winbinder_8php_afdd2d66a373514fe00f0d57d6bc4fb09}{wb\+\_\+sort()}} sorts the column indexed by subitem. The index of the first column is zero.

Returns T\+R\+UE on success or F\+A\+L\+SE if an error occurs.

 & {\em \$control} & \\
\hline
null & {\em \$ascending} & \\
\hline

\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wb\_wait()}{wb\_wait()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily wb\+\_\+wait (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$window = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$pause = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$flags = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This function creates a delay and verifies if mouse buttons are pressed and/or the keyboard state. This function is useful for lengthy operations. In this case, wb\+\_\+wait guarantees that the message control is sent back to the main loop, avoiding an unpleasant \char`\"{}freezing\char`\"{} effect. Using this function also provides an way to easily exit lengthy operations by constantly monitoring the keyboard and mouse.

Parameters\+: W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+D\+O\+WN W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+UP W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+D\+O\+WN W\+B\+C\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+UP
